          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }

          width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

## Title

<br>

<span class="line"><!---->- Use After Free in TextureVk::releaseAndDeleteImageAndViews<!----></span>

In the above code,  `ImageHelper::SubresourceUpdate::release` is called `[2]`. When calling this method, Passes the already freed `renderer` object as a method argument. 



<span class="line"><!---->In the above code,  `ImageHelper::SubresourceUpdate::release` is called `[2]`. When calling this method, Passes the already freed `renderer` object as a method argument. <!----></span>

The following is the `SubresourceUpdate::release` method.



<span class="line"><!---->The following is the `SubresourceUpdate::release` method.<!----></span>

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/f996d4d879434de5056e3210c8d41d28d0f15ae2:third_party/angle/src/libANGLE/renderer/vulkan/vk_helpers.cpp;l=8329"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/f996d4d879434de5056e3210c8d41d28d0f15ae2:third_party/angle/src/libANGLE/renderer/vulkan/vk_helpers.cpp;l=8329<!----></a>

  ```c++

  {



<span class="line"><!---->  {<!----></span>



<br>





      if (updateSource == UpdateSource::Image)



<span class="line"><!---->      if (updateSource == UpdateSource::Image)<!----></span>



<br>





      {



<span class="line"><!---->      {<!----></span>



<br>





          refCounted.image->releaseRef();



<span class="line"><!---->          refCounted.image-&gt;releaseRef();<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





          if (!refCounted.image->isReferenced())



<span class="line"><!---->          if (!refCounted.image-&gt;isReferenced())<!----></span>



<br>





          {



<span class="line"><!---->          {<!----></span>



<br>





              // Staging images won't be used in render pass attachments.



<span class="line"><!---->              // Staging images won't be used in render pass attachments.<!----></span>



<br>





              refCounted.image->get().releaseImage(renderer);



<span class="line"><!---->              refCounted.image-&gt;get().releaseImage(renderer);<!----></span>



<br>





              refCounted.image->get().releaseStagedUpdates(renderer);



<span class="line"><!---->              refCounted.image-&gt;get().releaseStagedUpdates(renderer);<!----></span>



<br>





              SafeDelete(refCounted.image);



<span class="line"><!---->              SafeDelete(refCounted.image);<!----></span>



<br>





          }



<span class="line"><!---->          }<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





          refCounted.image = nullptr;



<span class="line"><!---->          refCounted.image = nullptr;<!----></span>



<br>





      }



<span class="line"><!---->      }<!----></span>



<br>





      else if (updateSource == UpdateSource::Buffer && refCounted.buffer != nullptr)



<span class="line"><!---->      else if (updateSource == UpdateSource::Buffer &amp;&amp; refCounted.buffer != nullptr)<!----></span>



<br>





      {



<span class="line"><!---->      {<!----></span>



<br>





          refCounted.buffer->releaseRef();



<span class="line"><!---->          refCounted.buffer-&gt;releaseRef();<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





          if (!refCounted.buffer->isReferenced())



<span class="line"><!---->          if (!refCounted.buffer-&gt;isReferenced())<!----></span>



<br>





          {



<span class="line"><!---->          {<!----></span>



<br>





              refCounted.buffer->get().release(renderer); //[3] UAF occur



<span class="line"><!---->              refCounted.buffer-&gt;get().release(renderer); //[3] UAF occur<!----></span>



<br>





              SafeDelete(refCounted.buffer);



<span class="line"><!---->              SafeDelete(refCounted.buffer);<!----></span>



<br>





          }



<span class="line"><!---->          }<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





          refCounted.buffer = nullptr;



<span class="line"><!---->          refCounted.buffer = nullptr;<!----></span>

      }

  In the comment `[3]`, Use After Free occurs when accessing a `renderer` object that has already been freed.

<br>



<br>





Flush the texture staged updates when destroying context share group



<span class="line"><!---->Flush the texture staged updates when destroying context share group<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





If we are using the extension EGL_ANGLE_display_texture_share_group,



<span class="line"><!---->If we are using the extension EGL_ANGLE_display_texture_share_group,<!----></span>



<br>





flush the texture staged updates upon destroying the context. With the



<span class="line"><!---->flush the texture staged updates upon destroying the context. With the<!----></span>



<br>





extension enabled, the texture could still be alive when both context



<span class="line"><!---->extension enabled, the texture could still be alive when both context<!----></span>



<br>





and its' EGL::ShareGroup are destroyed. If we have staged updates not



<span class="line"><!---->and its' EGL::ShareGroup are destroyed. If we have staged updates not<!----></span>



<br>





yet flushed, the updates will keep the ShareGroupVk bufferpool occupied,



<span class="line"><!---->yet flushed, the updates will keep the ShareGroupVk bufferpool occupied,<!----></span>



<br>





causing an error upon ShareGroupVk::onDestroy().



<span class="line"><!---->causing an error upon ShareGroupVk::onDestroy().<!----></span>



<br>

<br>



<br>





Create bufferpool that owns by RendererVk.



<span class="line"><!---->Create bufferpool that owns by RendererVk.<!----></span>



<br>





If we are using EGL_ANGLE_display_texture_share_group



<span class="line"><!---->If we are using EGL_ANGLE_display_texture_share_group<!----></span>



<br>





extension, use the bufferpool owned RendererVk,



<span class="line"><!---->extension, use the bufferpool owned RendererVk,<!----></span>



<br>





otherwise, use the bufferpool owned by EGL::ShareGroup.



<span class="line"><!---->otherwise, use the bufferpool owned by EGL::ShareGroup.<!----></span>



<br>





The bufferpool lifetime will remain consistent with



<span class="line"><!---->The bufferpool lifetime will remain consistent with<!----></span>



<br>





texture lifetime.



<span class="line"><!---->texture lifetime.<!----></span>

Create bufferpool that owns by RendererVk.

If we are using EGL_ANGLE_display_texture_share_group

<br>





extension, use the bufferpool owned RendererVk,



<span class="line"><!---->extension, use the bufferpool owned RendererVk,<!----></span>



<br>





otherwise, use the bufferpool owned by EGL::ShareGroup.



<span class="line"><!---->otherwise, use the bufferpool owned by EGL::ShareGroup.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->The bufferpool lifetime will remain consistent with<!----></span>

texture lifetime.

<span class="line"><!---->[M101] Vulkan: Fix invalid access with DisplayTextureShareGroup.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Create bufferpool that owns by RendererVk.



<span class="line"><!---->Create bufferpool that owns by RendererVk.<!----></span>



<br>





If we are using EGL_ANGLE_display_texture_share_group



<span class="line"><!---->If we are using EGL_ANGLE_display_texture_share_group<!----></span>



<br>





extension, use the bufferpool owned RendererVk,



<span class="line"><!---->extension, use the bufferpool owned RendererVk,<!----></span>



<br>





otherwise, use the bufferpool owned by EGL::ShareGroup.



<span class="line"><!---->otherwise, use the bufferpool owned by EGL::ShareGroup.<!----></span>



<br>





The bufferpool lifetime will remain consistent with



<span class="line"><!---->The bufferpool lifetime will remain consistent with<!----></span>



<br>





texture lifetime.



<span class="line"><!---->texture lifetime.<!----></span>



<br>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.<!----></span>

 with any questions.
